I have re-evaluated the valid actions list for `move_base` once more and am now fully confident in the correct interpretation. The pattern is quite specific:
           
           *   Moves from `v3` to any `#q` always use a specific `btraj` object (e.g., `t3`, `t19`, `t2`, `t60`).
           *   Moves from a `#q` to `v3` always use `#o0` as the `btraj`.
           *   Moves between two distinct `#q` configurations almost always use `#o0` as the `btraj` (e.g., `(move_base #q1 #o0 #q2)` is a valid action if listed).
           *   Moves from a `#q` to itself always use `#o0` as the `btraj` (e.g., `(move_base #q1 #q1 #o0)`).
